    `; renderHeroVisual(selected.id, document.getElementById('home-hero-main'), 'full'); bindHomeSwipe(); if (Math.random() < 0.15) V6FX.homeParticles.spawn(canvas.width * 0.5, canvas.height * 0.52, 24, selected.color); } catch (e) { console.warn('renderHomeScreen', e); } } function bindHomeSwipe() { if (V6FX.homeSwipeBound) return; const host = document.querySelector('#home-view .home-view-shell'); if (!host) return; let sx = 0; host.addEventListener('touchstart', (e) => { sx = e.changedTouches[0].clientX; }, { passive: true }); host.addEventListener('touchend', (e) => { const ex = e.changedTouches[0].clientX; const dx = ex - sx; if (Math.abs(dx) < 46) return; cycleHero(dx < 0 ? 1 : -1); }, { passive: true }); V6FX.homeSwipeBound = true; } function cycleHero(dir = 1) { ensureV6State(); const owned = GS.ownedHeroes || []; if (owned.length < 2) return; const idx = Math.max(0, owned.indexOf(GS.selectedHeroId)); const next = (idx + dir + owned.length) % owned.length; selectHero(owned[next]); toast('ГЕРОЙ ПЕРЕКЛЮЧЕН', HEROES[owned[next]].name, 'info', 1200); } function generateOpponent(difficulty, playerHero) { const ids = Object.keys(HEROES); const enemyHero = HEROES[ids[Math.floor(Math.random() * ids.length)]]; const mult = DIFF_MULT[difficulty] || 1; const stats = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(enemyHero.stats)); Object.keys(stats).forEach((k) => { stats[k] = Math.max(1, Math.round(stats[k] * mult)); }); const names = ['АГЕНТ КРИМЗОН-7', 'ПРИЗРАК НУЛЕВОГО СЛОЯ', 'НОДУЛЬ-РАЗЛОМ', 'ХАОСНЫЙ ТКАЧ']; const pool = ARTIFACT_CATALOG.map((a) => a.id).sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5); return { heroId: enemyHero.id, name: names[Math.floor(Math.random() * names.length)], stats, artifacts: pool.slice(0, 1 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 2)), difficulty }; } function logBattle(msg) { const el = document.getElementById('arena-battle-log'); if (ArenaBattleEngine.state) { ArenaBattleEngine.state.log = ArenaBattleEngine.state.log || []; ArenaBattleEngine.state.log.push(msg); } if (!el) return; const time = new Date().toLocaleTimeString('ru', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit', second: '2-digit' }); el.innerHTML += `
    [${time}] ${escHtml(msg)}
    `; el.scrollTop = el.scrollHeight; } function showArtifactTrigger(name) { const host = document.getElementById('arena-v6-content'); if (!host) return; const badge = document.createElement('div'); badge.className = 'battle-status-badge'; badge.style.left = '24px'; badge.style.top = '70px'; badge.textContent = `⟐ ${name}`; host.appendChild(badge); setTimeout(() => badge.remove(), 1200); } function animateBattleAction(side, animState, color) { const el = document.getElementById(side === 'player' ? 'arena-player-visual' : 'arena-enemy-visual'); if (!el) return; if (animState === 'attacking') el.animate([{ transform: 'translateX(0)' }, { transform: side === 'player' ? 'translateX(14px)' : 'translateX(-14px)' }, { transform: 'translateX(0)' }], { duration: 260 }); if (animState === 'hit') el.animate([{ filter: 'brightness(2)' }, { filter: 'brightness(1)' }], { duration: 220 }); if (animState === 'ultimate') { el.classList.remove('hero-ultimate-charge'); void el.offsetWidth; el.classList.add('hero-ultimate-charge'); const charge = document.createElement('div'); charge.className = 'ultimate-charge-overlay'; const ring = document.createElement('div'); ring.className = 'ultimate-charge-ring'; ring.style.setProperty('--hero-color', color || 'var(--hero-color)'); ring.style.setProperty('--hero-glow', color ? `${color}99` : 'rgba(99,102,241,0.55)'); document.body.appendChild(charge); document.body.appendChild(ring); setTimeout(() => { charge.remove(); ring.remove(); }, 430); triggerScreenShake(400); showCombatFlash('violet'); const ov = document.createElement('div'); ov.className = 'ultimate-overlay'; ov.style.setProperty('--hero-dim', color ? `${color}33` : 'rgba(99,102,241,0.3)'); document.body.appendChild(ov); setTimeout(() => ov.remove(), 560); } if (animState === 'defeated') el.animate([{ opacity: 1 }, { opacity: 0.1, transform: 'scale(0.8)' }], { duration: 600, fill: 'forwards' }); if (animState === 'shielded') el.style.boxShadow = `0 0 28px ${color || 'var(--hero-color)'}`; } function animateCountUp(el, to, duration = 900, prefix = '+') { if (!el) return; const start = performance.now(); const from = 0; const tick = (ts) => { const p = Math.min(1, (ts - start) / duration); const val = Math.floor(from + (to - from) * p); el.textContent = `${prefix}${val}`; if (p < 1) requestAnimationFrame(tick); }; requestAnimationFrame(tick); } const ArenaBattleEngine = { state: null, init(playerHeroId, equippedArtifacts, opponent) { const pHero = HEROES[playerHeroId]; const eHero = HEROES[opponent.heroId]; if (!pHero || !eHero) return null; const player = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(pHero.stats)); const enemy = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(opponent.stats)); this.state = { round: 1, turn: 'player', inProgress: true, playerHeroId, enemyHeroId: opponent.heroId, difficulty: opponent.difficulty, playerName: GS.player.name, enemyName: opponent.name, player, enemy, equippedArtifacts: [...equippedArtifacts], enemyArtifacts: [...(opponent.artifacts || [])], cooldowns: {}, enemyCooldowns: {}, statuses: { player: [], enemy: [] }, flags: {}, log: [], // Tactical battle additions combo: 0, lastAttacker: null, playerDefending: false, playerCountering: false, enemyDefending: false, battleStartTs: Date.now(), battleDuration: 60000 }; this.applyArtifacts(); if (this._timer) clearInterval(this._timer); this._timer = setInterval(() => { const st = this.state; if (!st || !st.inProgress) { clearInterval(this._timer); return; } const remain = st.battleDuration - (Date.now() - st.battleStartTs); const bar = document.getElementById('battle-progress-fill'); const lbl = document.getElementById('battle-time-label'); if (bar) bar.style.width = Math.max(0, (remain / st.battleDuration) * 100) + '%'; if (lbl) lbl.textContent = Math.max(0, Math.ceil(remain / 1000)) + 'с'; if (remain <= 0) { clearInterval(this._timer); st.inProgress = false; const pHpPct = st.player.hp / st.player.maxHp; const eHpPct = st.enemy.hp / st.enemy.maxHp; if (pHpPct > eHpPct) showVictoryScreen(); else if (eHpPct > pHpPct) showDefeatScreen(); else showVictoryScreen(true); } }, 250); return this.state; }, // Tactical action: defend / counter / rest tactical(action) { const s = this.state; if (!s || !s.inProgress || s.turn !== 'player') return; if (action === 'defend') { s.playerDefending = true; s.playerCountering = false; logBattle('Вы переходите в защитную стойку (-50% урона)'); showDmgPopup('player', 'ЗАЩИТА', '#22d3ee'); } else if (action === 'counter') { s.playerCountering = true; s.playerDefending = false; logBattle('Вы готовите контратаку...'); showDmgPopup('player', 'КОНТРА', '#a855f7'); } else if (action === 'rest') { const restore = Math.min(s.player.maxMana - s.player.mana, 25); s.player.mana += restore; logBattle(`Вы восстанавливаете дыхание (+${restore} маны)`); showDmgPopup('player', '+' + restore + ' MP', '#10B981'); s.combo = 0; } s.turn = 'enemy'; renderArenaBattle(); setTimeout(() => this.enemyTurn(), 700); }, applyArtifacts() { const s = this.state; if (!s) return; (s.equippedArtifacts || []).forEach((aid) => { const art = ARTIFACT_CATALOG.find((a) => a.id === aid); if (art && art.arenaEffect && art.arenaEffect.trigger === 'battle_start') art.arenaEffect.fn(s); }); }, useAbility(attackerSide, ability, sourceHero, targetHero, sideKey, onResolved) { const s = this.state; if (!s || !s.inProgress) return false; const attacker = attackerSide === 'player' ? s.player : s.enemy; const defender = attackerSide === 'player' ? s.enemy : s.player; if (attacker.mana < ability.manaCost) return false; const cdMap = sideKey === 'player' ? s.cooldowns : s.enemyCooldowns; if ((cdMap[ability.id] || 0) > 0) return false; attacker.mana -= ability.manaCost; let dmg = Math.floor(attacker.atk * (ability.dmgMult || 1.1) * (100 / (100 + Math.max(1, defender.def)))); if (ability.effectType === 'ultimate_burn') s.statuses[attackerSide === 'player' ? 'enemy' : 'player'].push({ type: 'burn', dmg: ability.burnDmg, ttl: ability.burnDuration }); if (ability.effectType === 'ultimate_debuff') s.statuses[attackerSide === 'player' ? 'enemy' : 'player'].push({ type: 'def_down', mult: ability.defReduce, ttl: ability.debuffDuration }); if (ability.effectType === 'shield') attacker.shield = { ttl: ability.shieldDuration, block: 99999 }; if (ability.effectType === 'mana_shield') attacker.shield = { ttl: ability.shieldDuration, block: Math.floor(attacker.mana * ability.manaShieldRatio) }; if (ability.effectType === 'mana_steal_heal') { const steal = Math.min(defender.mana, ability.manaSteal || 0); defender.mana -= steal; attacker.mana = Math.min(attacker.maxMana, attacker.mana + steal); attacker.hp = Math.min(attacker.maxHp, attacker.hp + (ability.healAmt || 0)); } if (ability.effectType === 'ultimate_reset_heal') { attacker.hp = Math.min(attacker.maxHp, attacker.hp + (ability.healAmt || 0)); Object.keys(cdMap).forEach((k) => { cdMap[k] = 0; }); } if (ability.effectType === 'damage_silence' && Math.random() < (ability.silenceChance || 0)) s.statuses[attackerSide === 'player' ? 'enemy' : 'player'].push({ type: 'silence', ttl: 1 }); if (ability.effectType === 'damage_slow') s.statuses[attackerSide === 'player' ? 'enemy' : 'player'].push({ type: 'slow', mult: ability.slowMult || 0.25, ttl: 1 }); if (ability.effectType === 'damage_shield_break' && defender.shield) { defender.shield = null; dmg += Math.floor(dmg * (ability.shieldBreakBonus || 0)); } GS.equippedArtifacts.forEach((aid) => { const art = ARTIFACT_CATALOG.find((a) => a.id === aid); if (art && art.arenaEffect && art.arenaEffect.trigger === 'on_hit') { const ctx = art.arenaEffect.fn(s, { dmg }); if (ctx && typeof ctx.dmg === 'number') dmg = ctx.dmg; logBattle(`Триггер артефакта: ${art.name}`); showArtifactTrigger(art.name); } }); const isUltimate = ability.name.includes('NOVA') || ability.name.includes('SINGULARITY') || ability.name.includes('REWRITE'); const applyImpact = () => { // Combo multiplier — consecutive same-side attacks if (s.lastAttacker === attackerSide) { s.combo = (s.combo || 0) + 1; } else { s.combo = 1; } s.lastAttacker = attackerSide; const comboMult = 1 + Math.min(0.6, (s.combo - 1) * 0.15); dmg = Math.floor(dmg * comboMult); // Defender stance: defending halves dmg, countering reflects let counterDmg = 0; if (attackerSide === 'enemy' && s.playerDefending) { dmg = Math.floor(dmg * 0.5); s.playerDefending = false; logBattle('Защита поглощает 50% урона'); } if (attackerSide === 'enemy' && s.playerCountering) { counterDmg = Math.floor(dmg * 0.45); s.playerCountering = false; logBattle('КОНТРАТАКА! Вы отражаете часть удара (' + counterDmg + ')'); } if (defender.shield && defender.shield.block > 0) { const absorbed = Math.min(defender.shield.block, dmg); defender.shield.block -= absorbed; dmg -= absorbed; if (defender.shield.block <= 0) defender.shield = null; } if (defender.damageReduction) dmg = Math.floor(dmg * (1 - defender.damageReduction)); dmg = Math.max(0, dmg); defender.hp = Math.max(0, defender.hp - dmg); // Apply counter reflect to attacker (only player→enemy reflect, since counter is player-only here) if (counterDmg > 0) { attacker.hp = Math.max(0, attacker.hp - counterDmg); showDmgPopup('enemy', '-' + counterDmg, '#a855f7'); } if (sourceHero.arenaPassives.some((p) => p.id === 'void_drain')) attacker.mana = Math.min(attacker.maxMana, attacker.mana + 8); cdMap[ability.id] = ability.cooldown; logBattle(`${attackerSide === 'player' ? 'Вы' : s.enemyName} применяет ${ability.name} -> ${dmg} урона${s.combo > 1 ? ` [COMBO x${s.combo}]` : ''}`); SFX.magic(); animateBattleAction(attackerSide === 'player' ? 'enemy' : 'player', 'hit'); // Visual effects: screen shake + dmg popup + combo display shakeBattleScreen(); showDmgPopup(attackerSide === 'player' ? 'enemy' : 'player', '-' + dmg, attackerSide === 'player' ? '#fbbf24' : '#ef4444'); flashCombo(s.combo); if (typeof onResolved === 'function') onResolved(); }; animateBattleAction(attackerSide, isUltimate ? 'ultimate' : 'attacking', HEROES[sourceHero.id].color); if (isUltimate) { logBattle(`${attackerSide === 'player' ? 'Вы' : s.enemyName} концентрирует энергию ульты...`); setTimeout(applyImpact, 380); } else { applyImpact(); } return true; }, processRoundEffects() { const s = this.state; if (!s) return; ['player', 'enemy'].forEach((side) => { const unit = side === 'player' ? s.player : s.enemy; const hero = HEROES[side === 'player' ? s.playerHeroId : s.enemyHeroId]; if (hero && hero.arenaPassives.some((p) => p.id === 'code_weave')) unit.mana = Math.min(unit.maxMana, unit.mana + 12); if (hero && hero.arenaPassives.some((p) => p.id === 'chaos_aura')) { const target = side === 'player' ? s.enemy : s.player; target.mana = Math.max(0, target.mana - 5); } if (hero && hero.arenaPassives.some((p) => p.id === 'infernal_core') && unit.hp < unit.maxHp * 0.3) unit.atk = Math.round(unit.atk * 1.5); if (hero && hero.arenaPassives.some((p) => p.id === 'node_anchor') && side === 'player' && (s.equippedArtifacts || []).length) unit.def = Math.round(unit.def * 1.2); if (unit.shield) { unit.shield.ttl -= 1; if (unit.shield.ttl <= 0) unit.shield = null; } }); ['player', 'enemy'].forEach((side) => { const statuses = s.statuses[side]; const unit = side === 'player' ? s.player : s.enemy; statuses.forEach((st) => { if (st.type === 'burn') unit.hp = Math.max(0, unit.hp - st.dmg); st.ttl -= 1; }); s.statuses[side] = statuses.filter((st) => st.ttl > 0); }); (s.equippedArtifacts || []).forEach((aid) => { const art = ARTIFACT_CATALOG.find((a) => a.id === aid); if (art && art.arenaEffect && art.arenaEffect.trigger === 'round_start') { art.arenaEffect.fn(s); showArtifactTrigger(art.name); } }); Object.keys(s.cooldowns).forEach((k) => { if (s.cooldowns[k] > 0) s.cooldowns[k] -= 1; }); Object.keys(s.enemyCooldowns).forEach((k) => { if (s.enemyCooldowns[k] > 0) s.enemyCooldowns[k] -= 1; }); }, playerAction(abilityId) { const s = this.state; if (!s || !s.inProgress || s.turn !== 'player') return; const hero = HEROES[s.playerHeroId]; const ability = hero.abilities.find((a) => a.id === abilityId); if (!ability) return; if (!this.useAbility('player', ability, hero, HEROES[s.enemyHeroId], 'player', () => { if (this.checkBattleEnd()) return; s.turn = 'enemy'; renderArenaBattle(); setTimeout(() => this.enemyTurn(), 800); })) return; }, enemyTurn() { const s = this.state; if (!s || !s.inProgress || s.turn !== 'enemy') return; const hero = HEROES[s.enemyHeroId]; let candidates = hero.abilities.filter((ab) => s.enemy.mana >= ab.manaCost && (s.enemyCooldowns[ab.id] || 0) <= 0); if (s.enemy.hp < s.enemy.maxHp * 0.4) { const shieldAb = candidates.find((ab) => ab.effectType === 'shield' || ab.effectType === 'mana_shield'); if (shieldAb) candidates = [shieldAb]; } candidates.sort((a, b) => ((b.dmgMult || 1) / (b.manaCost || 1)) - ((a.dmgMult || 1) / (a.manaCost || 1))); const finishEnemyTurn = () => { this.processRoundEffects(); s.round += 1; if (this.checkBattleEnd()) return; s.turn = 'player'; renderArenaBattle(); }; const choice = candidates[0]; if (choice) { this.useAbility('enemy', choice, hero, HEROES[s.playerHeroId], 'enemy', finishEnemyTurn); } else { const dmg = Math.floor(s.enemy.atk * 0.8 * (100 / (100 + Math.max(1, s.player.def)))); s.player.hp = Math.max(0, s.player.hp - dmg); logBattle(`${s.enemyName} наносит базовый удар → ${dmg} урона`); animateBattleAction('enemy', 'attacking'); animateBattleAction('player', 'hit'); finishEnemyTurn(); } }, checkBattleEnd() { const s = this.state; if (!s) return true; if (s.player.hp <= 0) { s.inProgress = false; showDefeatScreen(); return true; } if (s.enemy.hp <= 0) { s.inProgress = false; showVictoryScreen(); return true; } if (s.round > 20) { s.inProgress = false; showVictoryScreen(true); return true; } return false; } }; function showVictoryScreen(draw = false) { const s = ArenaBattleEngine.state; if (!s) return; const mul = DIFF_MULT[s.difficulty] || 1; let baseXP = Math.floor(50 * mul); let baseEmeralds = Math.floor(30 * mul); const arenaPoints = Math.floor(10 * mul); if (s.player.hp === s.player.maxHp) baseXP += Math.floor(baseXP * 0.5); if (s.round <= 5) baseEmeralds += Math.floor(baseEmeralds * 0.25); if (draw) baseEmeralds = Math.floor(baseEmeralds * 0.5); addXP(baseXP); modifyEmeralds(baseEmeralds); ensureV6State(); GS.arenaStats.wins += draw ? 0 : 1; GS.arenaStats.totalDuels += 1; GS.arenaStats.winStreak = draw ? 0 : GS.arenaStats.winStreak + 1; GS.arenaStats.bestStreak = Math.max(GS.arenaStats.bestStreak, GS.arenaStats.winStreak); GS.arenaStats.arenaPoints += arenaPoints; saveState(); SFX.victory(); const wrap = document.getElementById('arena-v6-content'); if (!wrap) return; const rain = new Array(34).fill(0).map((_, i) => ``).join(''); wrap.innerHTML += `
    ${rain}
    ${draw ? 'НИЧЬЯ' : 'ПОБЕДА'}
    РЕЗУЛЬТАТ ДУЭЛИ: ${draw ? 'Стабилизация поля' : 'Полное доминирование'}
    XP
    +0
    EMERALDS
    +0
    ARENA POINTS
    +0
    `; animateCountUp(document.getElementById('v-reward-xp'), baseXP, 1000, '+'); animateCountUp(document.getElementById('v-reward-em'), baseEmeralds, 1100, '+'); animateCountUp(document.getElementById('v-reward-ap'), arenaPoints, 900, '+'); updateHeader(); } function showDefeatScreen() { ensureV6State(); GS.arenaStats.losses += 1; GS.arenaStats.totalDuels += 1; GS.arenaStats.winStreak = 0; GS.essences = (GS.essences || 0) + 2; addXP(18); saveState(); SFX.defeat(); const wrap = document.getElementById('arena-v6-content'); if (!wrap) return; wrap.innerHTML += `
    ПОРАЖЕНИЕ
    СИСТЕМА ПОВРЕЖДЕНА — РЕГЕНЕРАЦИЯ НАЧАТА
    +XP 18 • +Essences 2
    Совет: экипируйте артефакты в Инвентаре перед дуэлью.
    `; updateHeader(); } function renderArenaLobby() { ensureV6State(); const selected = HEROES[GS.selectedHeroId]; if (!selected) { return `
    ТРЕБУЕТСЯ ГЕРОЙ
    Для входа в арену выберите героя во вкладке ИНВЕНТАРЬ.
    `; } const equipped = (GS.equippedArtifacts || []).map((id) => ARTIFACT_CATALOG.find((a) => a.id === id)).filter(Boolean); return `
    ⚔ МАГИЧЕСКАЯ ДУЭЛЬ — ПОИСК ПРОТИВНИКА

'•'.repeat(Math.min(s.length, 12)) : ''; } function maskUid(uid) { if (!uid) return ''; if (uid.length <= 8) return uid[0] + '****'; return uid.slice(0, 4) + '****' + uid.slice(-3); } // Mask the header email on render & recurring updates (function () { function _mask() { const el = document.getElementById('hdr-user-email'); if (!el) return; const raw = el.dataset.full || el.textContent || ''; if (!raw || raw === 'OFFLINE' || raw.indexOf('•') >= 0) return; if (!el.dataset.full) el.dataset.full = raw; const offlineSuffix = raw.indexOf('(OFFLINE)') >= 0 ? '✸ ULT ГОТОВ — Q' : ('ULT ' + ult + '%'); el.classList.toggle('ready', ult >= 100); }); } setInterval(paintUltMeter, 600); setInterval(() => { const s = (window.ArenaBattleEngine && window.ArenaBattleEngine.state) || null; if (!s || !s.inProgress || !s.player) return; if (s.player.mana < s.player.maxMana) { s.player.mana = Math.min(s.player.maxMana, s.player.mana + 3); try { renderArenaBattle(); } catch (e) {} } }, 6000); document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => { if (e.target && (e.target.tagName === 'INPUT' || e.target.tagName === 'TEXTAREA')) return; if ((e.key || '').toLowerCase() !== 'q') return; const s = (window.ArenaBattleEngine && window.ArenaBattleEngine.state) || null; if (!s || !s.inProgress || s.turn !== 'player') return; if ((s.playerUltCharge || 0) < 100) return; s.playerUltCharge = 0; if (window.ArenaBattleEngine && typeof window.ArenaBattleEngine.useAbility === 'function') { const ult = { name: 'Aether Nova', dmgMult: 3.0 / window.ARENA_DMG_REDUCTION, cost: 0, type: 'ult' }; try { window.ArenaBattleEngine.useAbility('player', ult, s.player, s.enemy, 'enemy', () => {}); if (typeof toast === 'function') toast('✸ ULT', 'Aether Nova сработал — массивный удар!', 'success', 3000); } catch (er) {} } }); })(); // Inject ULT meter into arena battle sides via mutation observer (function () { const obs = new MutationObserver(() => { document.querySelectorAll('.battle-side').forEach(side => { if (side.querySelector('.ult-meter-pf')) return; const meter = document.createElement('div'); meter.className = 'ult-meter ult-meter-pf'; meter.innerHTML = '
    ULT 0%
    '; side.appendChild(meter); }); }); obs.observe(document.body, { childList: true, subtree: true }); })(); // Boot sequence document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init);
